    SELECT TOP(1) [c].[Id], [c].[AccessCode], [c].[AllowCodeReview], [c].[AllowMultipleAttempts], [c].[ApplyBreachRule], [c].[BreachRuleLimit], [c].[ClassId], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[CreatedBy], [c].[DurationMinutes], [c].[EndDate], [c].[HostIP], [c].[IsActive], [c].[IsPublished], [c].[IsResultPublishAutomatically], [c].[MaxAttempts], [c].[ShowResultsImmediately], [c].[StartDate], [c].[Tags], [c].[TestName], [c].[TestType], [c].[TotalMarks], [c].[TotalQuestions], [c].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [CodingTests] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [c2]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[CodingTestId], [c0].[CreatedAt], [c0].[CustomInstructions], [c0].[Marks], [c0].[ProblemId], [c0].[QuestionOrder], [c0].[TimeLimitMinutes], [p].[Id] AS [Id0], [p].[Constraints], [p].[Description], [p].[Difficulty], [p].[Examples], [p].[Hints], [p].[MemoryLimit], [p].[SubdomainId], [p].[TimeLimit], [p].[Title], [t].[Id] AS [Id1], [t].[ExpectedOutput], [t].[Input], [t].[ProblemId] AS [ProblemId0]
    FROM [CodingTestQuestions] AS [c0]
    INNER JOIN [Problems] AS [p] ON [c0].[ProblemId] = [p].[Id]
    LEFT JOIN [TestCases] AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProblemId]
) AS [s] ON [c2].[Id] = [s].[CodingTestId]
LEFT JOIN [CodingTestAttempts] AS [c1] ON [c2].[Id] = [c1].[CodingTestId]
ORDER BY [c2].[Id], [s].[Id], [s].[Id0], [s].[Id1]
